// Matrix Intelligence - –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–æ–π —Å–∫—Ä–∏–ø—Ç
class MatrixReport {
    constructor() {
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.loadMarketData();
        this.setupEventListeners();
        this.createInteractiveElements();
        console.log('Matrix Intelligence Report loaded');
    }

    // –ó–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞
    async loadMarketData() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('data/market-data.json');
            this.marketData = await response.json();
            this.renderMarketInsights();
        } catch (error) {
            console.log('–ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ–º –¥–µ–º–æ-–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ');
            this.loadDemoData();
        }
    }

    // –î–µ–º–æ-–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –µ—Å–ª–∏ JSON –Ω–µ –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∏–ª—Å—è
    loadDemoData() {
        this.marketData = {
            marketSize: {
                current: 45.2, // $45.2B
                growth: 18.5,  // 18.5% YoY
                forecast2027: 68.9
            },
            competition: {
                '360Learning': { marketShare: 12, growth: 25 },
                'Docebo': { marketShare: 18, growth: 15 },
                'Cornerstone': { marketShare: 22, growth: 8 },
                'LearnUpon': { marketShare: 9, growth: 20 }
            },
            trends: [
                { name: 'AI Learning', growth: 45 },
                { name: 'Collaborative', growth: 32 },
                { name: 'Microlearning', growth: 28 },
                { name: 'Mobile First', growth: 38 }
            ]
        };
        this.renderMarketInsights();
    }

    // –†–µ–Ω–¥–µ—Ä –∫–ª—é—á–µ–≤—ã—Ö –∏–Ω—Å–∞–π—Ç–æ–≤
    renderMarketInsights() {
        const insightsContainer = document.getElementById('market-dashboard');
        if (!insightsContainer) return;

        insightsContainer.innerHTML = `
            <section class="dashboard-section">
                <div class="dashboard-header">
                    <h3>üìä –ê–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞ L&D SaaS</h3>
                </div>
                
                <div class="metrics-grid">
                    <div class="metric-card">
                        <div class="metric-value">$${this.marketData.marketSize.current}B</div>
                        <div class="metric-label">–û–±—ä–µ–º —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞ 2025</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric-card">
                        <div class="metric-value">${this.marketData.marketSize.growth}%</div>
                        <div class="metric-label">–†–æ—Å—Ç YoY</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric-card">
                        <div class="metric-value">$${this.marketData.marketSize.forecast2027}B</div>
                        <div class="metric-label">–ü—Ä–æ–≥–Ω–æ–∑ 2027</div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="chart-container">
                    <div class="chart-placeholder">
                        üìà –ì—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω—Ç–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞ (–∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è...)
                    </div>
                </div>
            </section>
        `;
    }

    setupEventListeners() {
        // –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–æ—á–∫–∞–º –∏–Ω—Å–∞–π—Ç–æ–≤
        const insightCards = document.querySelectorAll('.insight-card');
        insightCards.forEach(card => {
            card.addEventListener('click', () => {
                this.toggleInsightDetail(card);
            });
        });
    }

    toggleInsightDetail(card) {
        card.classList.toggle('expanded');
    }

    createInteractiveElements() {
        // –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –∞–Ω–∏–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Å—á–µ—Ç—á–∏–∫–∏ –¥–ª—è –º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏–∫
        this.animateMetrics();
    }

    animateMetrics() {
        const metrics = document.querySelectorAll('.metric-value');
        metrics.forEach(metric => {
            this.animateValue(metric);
        });
    }

    animateValue(element) {
        // –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—è —á–∏—Å–µ–ª –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∞ –≤ charts.js
    }
}

// –ò–Ω–∏—Ü–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø—Ä–∏ –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü—ã
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    new MatrixReport();

javascript
// Matrix Intelligence - –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ –≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫–∏
class MatrixCharts {
    constructor(matrixReport) {
        this.report = matrixReport;
        this.initCharts();
    }

    initCharts() {
        this.createCompetitionChart();
        this.createTrendsChart();
        this.createGrowthChart();
    }

    // –ì—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω—Ç–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞
    createCompetitionChart() {
        const competitionData = this.report.marketData.competition;
        
        // –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–π–Ω–µ—Ä –¥–ª—è –≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫–∞
        const chartContainer = document.querySelector('.chart-placeholder');
        if (!chartContainer) return;

        chartContainer.innerHTML = `
            <div class="competition-chart">
                <h4>–î–æ–ª—è —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞ L&D SaaS (%)</h4>
                <div class="bars-container">
                    ${Object.entries(competitionData).map(([company, data]) => `
                        <div class="bar-item">
                            <div class="company-name">${company}</div>
                            <div class="bar-wrapper">
                                <div class="bar" style="width: ${data.marketShare}%; background: ${this.getCompanyColor(company)}">
                                    <span class="bar-value">${data.marketShare}%</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="growth">üìà ${data.growth}% —Ä–æ—Å—Ç</div>
                        </div>
                    `).join('')}
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    // –¶–≤–µ—Ç–∞ –¥–ª—è –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω–∏–π
    getCompanyColor(company) {
        const colors = {
            '360Learning': '#d97706', // matrix-gold
            'Docebo': '#1a365d',      // matrix-blue  
            'Cornerstone': '#38a169', // matrix-success
            'LearnUpon': '#6b46c1'    // purple
        };
        return colors[company] || '#718096';
    }

    // –ì—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫ —Ç—Ä–µ–Ω–¥–æ–≤ —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞
    createTrendsChart() {
        const trendsData = this.report.marketData.trends;
        
        // –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º —Å–µ–∫—Ü–∏—é –¥–ª—è —Ç—Ä–µ–Ω–¥–æ–≤
        const dashboardSection = document.querySelector('.dashboard-section');
        if (!dashboardSection) return;

        const trendsHTML = `
            <div class="chart-container">
                <h4>üöÄ –ö–ª—é—á–µ–≤—ã–µ —Ç—Ä–µ–Ω–¥—ã —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞</h4>
                <div class="trends-grid">
                    ${trendsData.map(trend => `
                        <div class="trend-item">
                            <div class="trend-name">${trend.name}</div>
                            <div class="trend-bar">
                                <div class="trend-value" style="width: ${trend.growth}%">
                                    ${trend.growth}% adoption
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    `).join('')}
                </div>
            </div>
        `;

        dashboardSection.innerHTML += trendsHTML;
    }

    // –ì—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫ —Ä–æ—Å—Ç–∞ —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞
    createGrowthChart() {
        const growthData = {
            years: [2020, 2021, 2022, 2023, 2024, 2025],
            marketSize: [25.1, 28.7, 32.4, 37.2, 41.8, 45.2],
            growthRate: [12.5, 14.3, 13.0, 14.8, 12.4, 18.5]
        };

        const growthHTML = `
            <div class="chart-container">
                <h4>üìà –î–∏–Ω–∞–º–∏–∫–∞ —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞ L&D (2020-2025)</h4>
                <div class="growth-chart">
                    <div class="growth-bars">
                        ${growthData.years.map((year, index) => `
                            <div class="growth-bar">
                                <div class="year">${year}</div>
                                <div class="size-bar" style="height: ${(growthData.marketSize[index] / 50) * 100}%">
                                    $${growthData.marketSize[index]}B
                                </div>
                                <div class="growth-rate">${growthData.growthRate[index]}%</div>
                            </div>
                        `).join('')}
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;

        // –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—â–∏—Ö –≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫–æ–≤
        const lastChart = document.querySelector('.chart-container:last-child');
        if (lastChart) {
            lastChart.insertAdjacentHTML('afterend', growthHTML);
        }
    }
}

// –ò–Ω–∏—Ü–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è –≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫–æ–≤ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∏ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–æ–≥–æ –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–∞
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    // –ñ–¥–µ–º –Ω–µ–º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –¥–ª—è –∏–Ω–∏—Ü–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–æ–≥–æ –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–∞
    setTimeout(() => {
        if (window.matrixReport) {
            new MatrixCharts(window.matrixReport);
        }
    }, 100);
});

// Matrix Intelligence - –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–æ–π —Å–∫—Ä–∏–ø—Ç (–∏—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è –≤–µ—Ä—Å–∏—è)
class MatrixReport {
    constructor() {
        this.marketData = this.getDemoData(); // –°—Ä–∞–∑—É –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ–º –¥–µ–º–æ-–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.renderMarketInsights();
        this.setupEventListeners();
        console.log('Matrix Intelligence Report loaded');
    }

    // –ü–æ–ª–Ω—ã–µ –¥–µ–º–æ-–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤ –∫–æ–¥–µ
    getDemoData() {
        return {
            marketSize: {
                current: 45.2,
                growth: 18.5,
                forecast2027: 68.9
            },
            competition: {
                '360Learning': { marketShare: 12, growth: 25 },
                'Docebo': { marketShare: 18, growth: 15 },
                'Cornerstone': { marketShare: 22, growth: 8 },
                'LearnUpon': { marketShare: 9, growth: 20 }
            },
            trends: [
                { name: 'AI Learning', growth: 45 },
                { name: 'Collaborative', growth: 32 },
                { name: 'Microlearning', growth: 28 },
                { name: 'Mobile First', growth: 38 }
            ]
        };
    }

    // –†–µ–Ω–¥–µ—Ä –∫–ª—é—á–µ–≤—ã—Ö –∏–Ω—Å–∞–π—Ç–æ–≤
    renderMarketInsights() {
        const insightsContainer = document.getElementById('market-dashboard');
        if (!insightsContainer) return;

        insightsContainer.innerHTML = `
            <section class="dashboard-section">
                <div class="dashboard-header">
                    <h3>üìä –ê–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞ L&D SaaS</h3>
                </div>
                
                <div class="metrics-grid">
                    <div class="metric-card">
                        <div class="metric-value">$${this.marketData.marketSize.current}B</div>
                        <div class="metric-label">–û–±—ä–µ–º —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞ 2025</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric-card">
                        <div class="metric-value">${this.marketData.marketSize.growth}%</div>
                        <div class="metric-label">–†–æ—Å—Ç YoY</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric-card">
                        <div class="metric-value">$${this.marketData.marketSize.forecast2027}B</div>
                        <div class="metric-label">–ü—Ä–æ–≥–Ω–æ–∑ 2027</div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <!-- –ö–æ–Ω–∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω—Ç–Ω—ã–π –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ -->
                <div class="chart-container">
                    <h4>üèÜ –î–æ–ª—è —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞ L&D SaaS (%)</h4>
                    <div class="bars-container">
                        ${Object.entries(this.marketData.competition).map(([company, data]) => `
                            <div class="bar-item">
                                <div class="company-name">${company}</div>
                                <div class="bar-wrapper">
                                    <div class="bar" style="width: ${data.marketShare}%; background: ${this.getCompanyColor(company)}">
                                        <span class="bar-value">${data.marketShare}%</span>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="growth">üìà ${data.growth}% —Ä–æ—Å—Ç</div>
                            </div>
                        `).join('')}
                    </div>
                </div>

                <!-- –¢—Ä–µ–Ω–¥—ã —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞ -->
                <div class="chart-container">
                    <h4>üöÄ –ö–ª—é—á–µ–≤—ã–µ —Ç—Ä–µ–Ω–¥—ã —Ä—ã–Ω–∫–∞</h4>
                    <div class="trends-grid">
                        ${this.marketData.trends.map(trend => `
                            <div class="trend-item">
                                <div class="trend-name">${trend.name}</div>
                                <div class="trend-bar">
                                    <div class="trend-value" style="width: ${trend.growth}%">
                                        ${trend.growth}% adoption
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        `).join('')}
                    </div>
                </div>
            </section>
        `;
    }

    // –¶–≤–µ—Ç–∞ –¥–ª—è –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω–∏–π
    getCompanyColor(company) {
        const colors = {
            '360Learning': '#d97706',
            'Docebo': '#1a365d',  
            'Cornerstone': '#38a169',
            'LearnUpon': '#6b46c1'
        };
        return colors[company] || '#718096';
    }

    setupEventListeners() {
        // –ò–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–æ—á–µ–∫
        const insightCards = document.querySelectorAll('.insight-card');
        insightCards.forEach(card => {
            card.addEventListener('click', () => {
                card.classList.toggle('expanded');
            });
        });
    }
}

// –ò–Ω–∏—Ü–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø—Ä–∏ –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü—ã

üß† Recommended Report Structure (English Format)
Here‚Äôs a typical structure used in English-language market research reports:
Title Page Company name, report title, date, author.
Executive Summary Key findings, recommendations, and business implications.
Research Objectives What questions the report aims to answer.
Methodology Data sources, sample size, research tools.
Market Overview Size, growth rate, segmentation, trends.
Target Audience Analysis Demographics, psychographics, behavior.
Competitive Landscape Key players, SWOT analysis, market share.
Insights & Recommendations Strategic suggestions based on findings.
Appendices Charts, raw data, survey instruments.

(English Format) Here‚Äôs a typical structure used in English-language market research reports: 1. Title Page Company name, report title, date, author. 2. Executive Summary Key findings, recommendations, and business implications. 3. Research Objectives What questions the report aims to answer. 4. Methodology Data sources, sample size, research tools. 5. Market Overview Size, growth rate, segmentation, trends. 6. Target Audience Analysis Demographics, psychographics, behavior. 7. Competitive Landscape Key players, SWOT analysis, market share. 8. Insights & Recommendations Strategic suggestions based on findings. 9. ‚ö° 3. –§–ê–ô–õ: js/main.js
javascript
// Matrix Intelligence Dashboard - Main Controller
class MatrixIntelligenceDashboard {
    constructor() {
        this.metrics = {};
        this.updateFrequency = 'monthly';
        this.isLive = true;
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.bindEvents();
        this.loadInitialData();
        this.startLiveUpdates();
    }

    bindEvents() {
        // Update frequency control
        document.getElementById('update-frequency').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            this.setUpdateFrequency(e.target.value);
        });

        // Request changes button
        document.getElementById('request-changes').addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.showChangeRequestModal();
        });

        // Download PDF
        document.getElementById('download-pdf').addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.generatePDFReport();
        });

        // Subscription buttons
        document.querySelectorAll('.btn-primary').forEach(btn => {
            if (btn.textContent.includes('USDT')) {
                btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    this.processSubscription();
                });
            }
        });
    }

    setUpdateFrequency(frequency) {
        this.updateFrequency = frequency;
        this.showNotification(`Update frequency set to: ${frequency}`);
        // In production: Send to backend API
    }

    showChangeRequestModal() {
        const changeRequest = prompt('What changes would you like to request?');
        if (changeRequest) {
            this.submitChangeRequest(changeRequest);
        }
    }

    submitChangeRequest(request) {
        // Simulate API call
        console.log('Change request submitted:', request);
        this.showNotification('Change request submitted successfully');
        
        // In production: Send to backend
        // fetch('/api/change-requests', {
        //     method: 'POST',
        //     body: JSON.stringify({ request })
        // });
    }

    loadInitialData() {
        // Simulate loading real data
        setTimeout(() => {
            this.updateMetric('market-share', '32.4%', '+2.1% from last month');
            this.updateMetric('budget-trends', '$2.1B', 'Growing at 15% YoY');
            this.updateMetric('ai-adoption', '67%', '+28% in Q3 2025');
            this.updateMetric('competition', '4.2/5.0', 'Leading in innovation');
        }, 1000);
    }

    updateMetric(metricId, value, trend) {
        const valueElement = document.getElementById(`${metricId}-value`);
        const trendElement = document.getElementById(`${metricId}-trend`);
        
        if (valueElement) valueElement.textContent = value;
        if (trendElement) trendElement.textContent = trend;
    }

    startLiveUpdates() {
        // Simulate live data updates
        setInterval(() => {
            if (this.isLive) {
                this.simulateLiveDataUpdate();
            }
        }, 30000); // Every 30 seconds
    }

    simulateLiveDataUpdate() {
        const metrics = ['market-share', 'budget-trends', 'ai-adoption', 'competition'];
        const randomMetric = metrics[Math.floor(Math.random() * metrics.length)];
        
        // Small random fluctuations for demo
        const fluctuations = {
            'market-share': ['32.3%', '32.5%', '32.4%'],
            'budget-trends': ['$2.09B', '$2.11B', '$2.1B'],
            'ai-adoption': ['66%', '67%', '68%'],
            'competition': ['4.1/5.0', '4.2/5.0', '4.3/5.0']
        };
        
        const newValue = fluctuations[randomMetric][Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)];
        this.updateMetric(randomMetric, newValue, 'Live update');
    }

    generatePDFReport() {
        this.showNotification('Generating PDF report...');
        // In production: Call PDF generation API
        // fetch('/api/generate-pdf')
    }

    processSubscription() {
        const usdtAddress = 'TYMHG9jvnm2wNnA6fq5h7Z1aQaC6k4E5zX';
        this.showNotification(`Please send USDT to: ${usdtAddress}`);
        
        // In production: Integrate with payment processor
    }

    showNotification(message) {
        // Simple notification - can be enhanced with toast library
        alert(`Matrix Intelligence: ${message}`);
    }
}

// Initialize dashboard when DOM is loaded
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    window.dashboard = new MatrixIntelligenceDashboard();
});

üìä 4. –§–ê–ô–õ: js/metrics.js
javascript
// Advanced Metrics System for Matrix Intelligence
class MetricsEngine {
    constructor() {
        this.dataSources = [
            'L&D Market Reports',
            'Competitor Analysis',
            'Industry Trends',
            'Customer Feedback',
            'Technology Adoption Data'
        ];
        this.metricDefinitions = {
            'market-share': {
                name: 'Market Share Dynamics',
                description: 'Real-time market position tracking',
                sources: ['L&D Market Reports', 'Competitor Analysis'],
                updateInterval: 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 // 24 hours
            },
            'budget-trends': {
                name: 'L&D Budget Trends',
                description: 'Enterprise spending patterns and forecasts',
                sources: ['Industry Trends', 'Customer Feedback'],
                updateInterval: 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 // 7 days
            },
            'ai-adoption': {
                name: 'AI Adoption Rate',
                description: 'Technology integration progress across industry',
                sources: ['Technology Adoption Data', 'Industry Trends'],
                updateInterval: 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 // 24 hours
            },
            'competition': {
                name: 'Competitive Analysis',
                description: 'Comprehensive competitor intelligence',
                sources: ['Competitor Analysis', 'Customer Feedback'],
                updateInterval: 3 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 // 3 days
            }
        };
    }

    // Method to simulate API data fetching
    async fetchMetricData(metricId) {
        // Simulate API delay
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
        
        const mockData = {
            'market-share': {
                value: '32.4%',
                trend: '+2.1% from last month',
                confidence: 0.95,
                lastUpdated: new Date().toISOString()
            },
            'budget-trends': {
                value: '$2.1B',
                trend: 'Growing at 15% YoY',
                confidence: 0.88,
                lastUpdated: new Date().toISOString()
            },
            'ai-adoption': {
                value: '67%',
                trend: '+28% in Q3 2025',
                confidence: 0.92,
                lastUpdated: new Date().toISOString()
            },
            'competition': {
                value: '4.2/5.0',
                trend: 'Leading in innovation',
                confidence: 0.85,
                lastUpdated: new Date().toISOString()
            }
        };

        return mockData[metricId] || { value: 'N/A', trend: 'Data unavailable' };
    }

    // Advanced metric calculations
    calculateTrend(current, previous) {
        if (!previous || previous === 0) return 'New metric';
        const change = ((current - previous) / previous) * 100;
        return change >= 0 ? `+${change.toFixed(1)}%` : `${change.toFixed(1)}%`;
    }

    // Data validation and quality scoring
    validateDataQuality(data) {
        const checks = {
            timeliness: data.lastUpdated ? 
                (Date.now() - new Date(data.lastUpdated).getTime()) < 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 : false,
            completeness: data.value && data.trend,
            confidence: data.confidence > 0.8
        };
        
        const score = Object.values(checks).filter(Boolean).length / Object.keys(checks).length;
        return { checks, score };
    }
}

// Initialize metrics engine
const metricsEngine = new MetricsEngine();

// Export for use in main.js (if using modules)
if (typeof module !== 'undefined' && module.exports) {
    module.exports = { MetricsEngine, metricsEngine };
}

markdown
# 360Learning Matrix Intelligence Dashboard

## üöÄ Live L&D Market Monitoring Organism

### Quick Start
1. Open `index.html` in a web browser
2. View live market metrics
3. Use control panel to manage monitoring frequency
4. Access subscription options

### Features
- ‚úÖ Real-time market metrics for L&D industry
- ‚úÖ Adaptive update frequency controls
- ‚úÖ Change request system
- ‚úÖ PDF report generation
- ‚úÖ USDT subscription payments

### File Structure
360learning-matrix-intelligence/
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ index.html # Main dashboard
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ css/
‚îÇ ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ style.css # Matrix Intelligence design system
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ js/
‚îÇ ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ main.js # Dashboard controller
‚îÇ ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ metrics.js # Advanced metrics engine
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ README.md # This file
text

### Customization
- Update metrics in `js/metrics.js`
- Modify styling in `css/style.css`
- Integrate real APIs in `js/main.js`

### Deployment
Ready for GitHub Pages deployment. Simply push to repository and enable Pages in settings.

// –í —Ñ–∞–π–ª js/main.js –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º PDF –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—é
class PDFReportSystem {
    constructor() {
        this.reportTemplates = {
            'executive-summary': '–®–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω –¥–ª—è –∫—Ä–∞—Ç–∫–æ–≥–æ –æ–±–∑–æ—Ä–∞',
            'full-analysis': '–®–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω –ø–æ–ª–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞',
            'competitive-intel': '–®–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω –∫–æ–Ω–∫—É—Ä–µ–Ω—Ç–Ω–æ–π —Ä–∞–∑–≤–µ–¥–∫–∏'
        };
    }

    generatePDFReport(reportType, clientData) {
        // –ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è —Å –±–∏–±–ª–∏–æ—Ç–µ–∫–æ–π –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ PDF
        const reportData = this.prepareReportData(reportType, clientData);
        return this.downloadPDF(reportData);
    }

    prepareReportData(reportType, clientData) {
        return {
            title: `Matrix Intelligence Report - ${clientData.companyName}`,
            sections: this.reportTemplates[reportType],
            data: clientData.metrics,
            generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
            brand: 'Matrix Intelligence'
        };
    }

    downloadPDF(reportData) {
        // –ó–∞–≥–ª—É—à–∫–∞ –¥–ª—è —Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–π PDF –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏
        console.log('Generating PDF:', reportData);
        return `pdf-report-${Date.now()}.pdf`;
    }
}
2. –ò–ù–¢–ï–ì–†–ê–¶–ò–Ø –° –õ–ï–ù–î–ò–ù–ì–û–ú
javascript
// –ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è –∫–Ω–æ–ø–æ–∫ PDF –≤ —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—â–∏–π –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å
function integratePDFFeatures() {
    // –ö–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∞ —Å–∫–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è PDF
    const downloadBtn = document.getElementById('download-pdf');
    if (downloadBtn) {
        downloadBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            const pdfSystem = new PDFReportSystem();
            const pdfUrl = await pdfSystem.generatePDFReport(
                'executive-summary', 
                window.clientData
            );
            triggerPDFDownload(pdfUrl);
        });
    }

    // –ö–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∞ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–∞
    const updateBtn = document.getElementById('request-update');
    if (updateBtn) {
        updateBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            requestReportUpdate();
        });
    }
}

function triggerPDFDownload(pdfUrl) {
    // –°–∏–º—É–ª—è—Ü–∏—è —Å–∫–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è PDF
    const link = document.createElement('a');
    link.href = pdfUrl;
    link.download = `360Learning-Matrix-Report-${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.pdf`;
    link.click();
}

function requestReportUpdate() {
    // –°–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∞ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–∞
    const updateReason = prompt('–ß—Ç–æ –≤—ã —Ö–æ—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ç—å –≤ –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–µ?');
    if (updateReason) {
        // –û—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∫–∞ –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∞ –Ω–∞ –±—ç–∫–µ–Ω–¥
        console.log('Report update requested:', updateReason);
        showNotification('–ó–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å –Ω–∞ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–∞ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω');
    }
}

üîÑ 3. –°–ò–°–¢–ï–ú–ê –°–ò–ù–•–†–û–ù–ò–ó–ê–¶–ò–ò –î–ê–ù–ù–´–•
javascript
// –í —Ñ–∞–π–ª js/metrics.js –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é
class DataSynchronizer {
    constructor() {
        this.pdfData = null;
        this.liveData = null;
        this.lastSync = null;
    }

    // –°–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –º–µ–∂–¥—É PDF –∏ –ª–µ–Ω–¥–∏–Ω–≥–æ–º
    syncPDFWithDashboard(pdfReport, liveMetrics) {
        this.pdfData = this.extractPDFData(pdfReport);
        this.liveData = this.prepareLiveData(liveMetrics);
        this.lastSync = new Date();
        
        return this.createUnifiedDataModel();
    }

    extractPDFData(pdfReport) {
        // –ò–∑–≤–ª–µ—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –∏–∑ PDF
        return {
            marketAnalysis: pdfReport.sections?.marketAnalysis || {},
            recommendations: pdfReport.sections?.recommendations || [],
            generatedDate: pdfReport.generatedAt
        };
    }

    prepareLiveData(liveMetrics) {
        // –ü–æ–¥–≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∫–∞ live –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –¥–ª—è —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏
        return {
            currentMetrics: liveMetrics,
            lastUpdated: new Date().toISOString(),
            updateSchedule: window.dashboard?.updateFrequency || 'monthly'
        };
    }

    createUnifiedDataModel() {
        return {
            staticReport: this.pdfData,
            liveMonitoring: this.liveData,
            synchronization: {
                lastSync: this.lastSync,
                status: 'active',
                nextUpdate: this.calculateNextUpdate()
            }
        };
    }

    calculateNextUpdate() {
        const frequency = window.dashboard?.updateFrequency || 'monthly';
        const nextUpdate = new Date();
        
        switch(frequency) {
            case 'monthly':
                nextUpdate.setMonth(nextUpdate.getMonth() + 1);
                break;
            case 'quarterly':
                nextUpdate.setMonth(nextUpdate.getMonth() + 3);
                break;
            default:
                nextUpdate.setDate(nextUpdate.getDate() + 7);
        }
        
        return nextUpdate.toISOString();
    }
}

async function loadInitialReportData() {
    // –°–∏–º—É–ª—è—Ü–∏—è –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–∞

        companyName: '360Learning',
        metrics: window.metricsEngine?.metricDefinitions || {},
        generatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
    };
    
    window.clientData = sampleReport;
    updateSyncStatus();
}

function updateSyncStatus() {
    const syncTime = document.getElementById('last-update-time');
    if (syncTime) {
        syncTime.textContent = new Date().toLocaleString();
    }
}

‚ö° 4. JavaScript –î–õ–Ø –§–£–ù–ö–¶–ò–û–ù–ê–õ–ê
javascript
// PDF and Upgrade functionality
function downloadPDFReport() {
    // –í —Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–π —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∑–¥–µ—Å—å –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è PDF
    const pdfContent = document.querySelector('.pdf-demonstration').innerHTML;
    
    // –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—É—é —Å—Å—ã–ª–∫—É –¥–ª—è —Å–∫–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è
    const blob = new Blob([pdfContent], { type: 'text/markdown' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    
    a.href = url;
    a.download = 'matrix-intelligence-360learning-report.md';
    document.body.appendChild(a);
    a.click();
    document.body.removeChild(a);
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    
    showNotification('PDF –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤ –∫ —Å–∫–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–Ω–∏—é');
}

function showLiveDemo() {
    // –ü–µ—Ä–µ—Ö–æ–¥ –∫ –∂–∏–≤–æ–π –¥–µ–º–æ-–≤–µ—Ä—Å–∏–∏ –¥–∞—à–±–æ—Ä–¥–∞
    document.querySelector('.metrics').scrollIntoView({ 
        behavior: 'smooth' 
    });
    
    // –ê–∫—Ç–∏–≤–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –¥–µ–º–æ-—Ä–µ–∂–∏–º
    window.dashboard.activateDemoMode();
}

function startUpgradeProcess() {
    // –ò–Ω–∏—Ü–∏–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å –∞–ø–≥—Ä–µ–π–¥–∞
    const upgradeData = {
        currentPlan: 'pdf_report',
        targetPlan: 'matrix_intelligence',
        company: '360Learning',
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    };
    
    // –í —Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–π —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ - –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ –±—ç–∫–µ–Ω–¥
    console.log('Upgrade process started:', upgradeData);
    showNotification('–ü—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å –∞–ø–≥—Ä–µ–π–¥–∞ –∫ Matrix Intelligence –∑–∞–ø—É—â–µ–Ω!');
}

function requestConsultation() {
    // –ó–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å –∫–æ–Ω—Å—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ü–∏–∏
    const contactInfo = prompt('–û—Å—Ç–∞–≤—å—Ç–µ –≤–∞—à email –∏–ª–∏ —Ç–µ–ª–µ—Ñ–æ–Ω –¥–ª—è –∫–æ–Ω—Å—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ü–∏–∏:');
    if (contactInfo) {
        // –í —Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–π —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ - –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ –±—ç–∫–µ–Ω–¥
        console.log('Consultation requested:', contactInfo);
        showNotification('–°–ø–∞—Å–∏–±–æ! –ù–∞—à —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏–∞–ª–∏—Å—Ç —Å–≤—è–∂–µ—Ç—Å—è —Å –≤–∞–º–∏ –≤ —Ç–µ—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ 24 —á–∞—Å–æ–≤.');
    }
}

// –ò–Ω–∏—Ü–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø—Ä–∏ –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–µ
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—á–∏–∫–∏ –¥–ª—è –Ω–æ–≤—ã—Ö –∫–Ω–æ–ø–æ–∫
    const downloadBtn = document.querySelector('.btn-download-pdf');
    const liveDemoBtn = document.querySelector('.btn-live-demo');
    const upgradeBtn = document.querySelector('.btn-upgrade');
    const consultationBtn = document.querySelector('.btn-consultation');
    
    if (downloadBtn) downloadBtn.addEventListener('click', downloadPDFReport);
    if (liveDemoBtn) liveDemoBtn.addEventListener('click', showLiveDemo);
    if (upgradeBtn) upgradeBtn.addEventListener('click', startUpgradeProcess);
    if (consultationBtn) consultationBtn.addEventListener('click', requestConsultation);
});

üé® css/style.css (–æ—Å—Ç–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –±–µ–∑ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–π, —Ç–∞–∫ –∫–∞–∫ —É–∂–µ –Ω–∞ –∞–Ω–≥–ª–∏–π—Å–∫–æ–º)
‚ö° js/main.js (–æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è –∞–Ω–≥–ª–∏–π—Å–∫–∞—è –≤–µ—Ä—Å–∏—è)
javascript
// Matrix Intelligence Dashboard - Main Controller (English Version)
class MatrixIntelligenceDashboard {
    constructor() {
        this.metrics = {};
        this.updateFrequency = 'monthly';
        this.isLive = true;
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.bindEvents();
        this.loadInitialData();
        this.startLiveUpdates();
        this.integratePDFFeatures();
    }

    bindEvents() {
        // Update frequency control
        document.getElementById('update-frequency').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            this.setUpdateFrequency(e.target.value);
        });

        // Request changes button
        document.getElementById('request-changes').addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.showChangeRequestModal();
        });

        // Download PDF
        document.getElementById('download-pdf').addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.generatePDFReport();
        });

        // Subscription buttons
        document.querySelectorAll('.btn-primary').forEach(btn => {
            if (btn.textContent.includes('USDT')) {
                btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    this.processSubscription();
                });
            }
        });
    }

    integratePDFFeatures() {
        const downloadBtn = document.querySelector('.btn-download-pdf');
        const liveDemoBtn = document.querySelector('.btn-live-demo');
        const upgradeBtn = document.querySelector('.btn-upgrade');
        const consultationBtn = document.querySelector('.btn-consultation');
        
        if (downloadBtn) downloadBtn.addEventListener('click', this.downloadPDFReport);
        if (liveDemoBtn) liveDemoBtn.addEventListener('click', this.showLiveDemo);
        if (upgradeBtn) upgradeBtn.addEventListener('click', this.startUpgradeProcess);
        if (consultationBtn) consultationBtn.addEventListener('click', this.requestConsultation);
    }

    downloadPDFReport() {
        // In real implementation - PDF generation
        const pdfContent = `MATRIX INTELLIGENCE REPORT\nL&D Market Analysis for 360Learning\n\nFull report structure is ready.\nSpecific data will be added after conducting unique research.`;
        
        const blob = new Blob([pdfContent], { type: 'text/markdown' });
        const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        
        a.href = url;
        a.download = 'matrix-intelligence-360learning-report.md';
        document.body.appendChild(a);
        a.click();
        document.body.removeChild(a);
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
        
        this.showNotification('PDF report is ready for download');
    }

    showLiveDemo() {
        document.querySelector('.metrics').scrollIntoView({ 
            behavior: 'smooth' 
        });
        this.activateDemoMode();
    }

    startUpgradeProcess() {
        const upgradeData = {
            currentPlan: 'pdf_report',
            targetPlan: 'matrix_intelligence',
            company: '360Learning',
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        };
        
        console.log('Upgrade process started:', upgradeData);
        this.showNotification('Upgrade process to Matrix Intelligence started!');
    }

    requestConsultation() {
        const contactInfo = prompt('Please provide your email or phone for consultation:');
        if (contactInfo) {
            console.log('Consultation requested:', contactInfo);
            this.showNotification('Thank you! Our specialist will contact you within 24 hours.');
        }
    }

    setUpdateFrequency(frequency) {
        this.updateFrequency = frequency;
        this.showNotification(`Update frequency set to: ${frequency}`);
    }

    showChangeRequestModal() {
        const changeRequest = prompt('What changes would you like to request?');
        if (changeRequest) {
            this.submitChangeRequest(changeRequest);
        }
    }

    submitChangeRequest(request) {
        console.log('Change request submitted:', request);
        this.showNotification('Change request submitted successfully');
    }

    loadInitialData() {
        setTimeout(() => {
            this.updateMetric('market-share', '32.4%', '+2.1% from last month');
            this.updateMetric('budget-trends', '$2.1B', 'Growing at 15% YoY');
            this.updateMetric('ai-adoption', '67%', '+28% in Q3 2025');
            this.updateMetric('competition', '4.2/5.0', 'Leading in innovation');
        }, 1000);
    }

    updateMetric(metricId, value, trend) {
        const valueElement = document.getElementById(`${metricId}-value`);
        const trendElement = document.getElementById(`${metricId}-trend`);
        
        if (valueElement) valueElement.textContent = value;
        if (trendElement) trendElement.textContent = trend;
    }

    startLiveUpdates() {
        setInterval(() => {
            if (this.isLive) {
                this.simulateLiveDataUpdate();
            }
        }, 30000);
    }

    simulateLiveDataUpdate() {
        const metrics = ['market-share', 'budget-trends', 'ai-adoption', 'competition'];
        const randomMetric = metrics[Math.floor(Math.random() * metrics.length)];
        
        const fluctuations = {
            'market-share': ['32.3%', '32.5%', '32.4%'],
            'budget-trends': ['$2.09B', '$2.11B', '$2.1B'],
            'ai-adoption': ['66%', '67%', '68%'],
            'competition': ['4.1/5.0', '4.2/5.0', '4.3/5.0']
        };
        
        const newValue = fluctuations[randomMetric][Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)];
        this.updateMetric(randomMetric, newValue, 'Live update');
    }

    generatePDFReport() {
        this.showNotification('Generating PDF report...');
    }

    processSubscription() {
        const usdtAddress = 'TYMHG9jvnm2wNnA6fq5h7Z1aQaC6k4E5zX';
        this.showNotification(`Please send USDT to: ${usdtAddress}`);
    }

    activateDemoMode() {
        this.showNotification('Demo mode activated. Showing live metrics simulation.');
    }

    showNotification(message) {
        // Simple notification - can be enhanced with toast library
        alert(`Matrix Intelligence: ${message}`);
    }
}

// Initialize dashboard when DOM is loaded
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    window.dashboard = new MatrixIntelligenceDashboard();
});

profile-landing.js:
javascript
// Profile Landing Page Functionality
class ProfileLanding {
    constructor() {
        this.selectedFormat = null;
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.bindEvents();
    }

    bindEvents() {
        // Format selection
        document.querySelectorAll('.format-card button').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                const format = e.target.closest('.format-card').querySelector('h3').textContent;
                this.selectFormat(format);
            });
        });

        // Payment confirmation
        const confirmBtn = document.querySelector('.btn-confirm');
        if (confirmBtn) {
            confirmBtn.addEventListener('click', this.showConfirmationForm);
        }
    }

    requestDemo() {
        const company = prompt('Please enter your company name:');
        const email = prompt('Please enter your email for demo delivery:');
        
        if (company && email) {
            this.submitDemoRequest(company, email);
        }
    }

    submitDemoRequest(company, email) {
        // In production: Send to backend
        const requestData = {
            company: company,
            email: email,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            source: 'profile_landing'
        };

        console.log('Demo request submitted:', requestData);
        this.showNotification('Demo request received! We will contact you within 24 hours.');
        
        // Simulate demo delivery
        setTimeout(() => {
            this.deliverDemoReport(company, email);
        }, 2000);
    }

    deliverDemoReport(company, email) {
        // In production: Generate and send actual demo
        const demoContent = this.generateDemoContent(company);
        
        // Simulate email delivery
        console.log('Demo report delivered to:', email);
        this.showNotification(`Demo report sent to ${email}! Check your inbox.`);
    }

    generateDemoContent(company) {
        return {
            company: company,
            sections: [
                "Market Overview Analysis",
                "Competitive Landscape", 
                "Target Audience Insights",
                "Strategic Recommendations",
                "Implementation Roadmap"
            ],
            generated: new Date().toISOString()
        };
    }

    selectFormat(format) {
        this.selectedFormat = format;
        document.getElementById('payment').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
        this.showNotification(`Selected: ${format}. Proceed to payment when ready.`);
    }

    copyAddress() {
        const address = document.getElementById('usdt-address').textContent;
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(address).then(() => {
            this.showNotification('USDT address copied to clipboard!');
        });
    }

    showConfirmationForm() {
        const txHash = prompt('Please enter your USDT transaction hash:');
        const email = prompt('Please enter your email for report delivery:');
        
        if (txHash && email) {
            this.confirmPayment(txHash, email);
        }
    }

    confirmPayment(txHash, email) {
        const paymentData = {
            format: this.selectedFormat,
            txHash: txHash,
            email: email,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        };

        console.log('Payment confirmed:', paymentData);
        this.showNotification('Payment confirmed! Full report will be delivered within 48 hours.');
        
        // In production: Trigger report generation and delivery
    }

    showNotification(message) {
        // Simple notification - can be enhanced with toast library
        const notification = document.createElement('div');
        notification.style.cssText = `
            position: fixed;
            top: 20px;
            right: 20px;
            background: var(--matrix-accent);
            color: var(--matrix-bg);
            padding: 1rem 1.5rem;
            border-radius: 8px;
            z-index: 10000;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 25px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
        `;
        notification.textContent = message;
        document.body.appendChild(notification);
        
        setTimeout(() => {
            document.body.removeChild(notification);
        }, 5000);
    }
}

// Initialize when DOM is loaded
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    window.profileLanding = new ProfileLanding();
});

// Global functions for HTML onclick handlers
function requestDemo() {
    window.profileLanding.requestDemo();
}

function scrollToHowItWorks() {
    document.getElementById('how-it-works').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
}

function selectFormat(format) {
    window.profileLanding.selectFormat(format);
}

function copyAddress() {
    window.profileLanding.copyAddress();
}

function showConfirmationForm() {
    window.profileLanding.showConfirmationForm();
}
pulse-dashboard.js:
javascript
// Pulse Dashboard Functionality
class PulseDashboard {
    constructor() {
        this.metrics = {};
        this.isSubscribed = false;
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.checkSubscription();
        this.bindEvents();
        this.loadDemoMetrics();
    }

    checkSubscription() {
        // In production: Check user subscription status
        this.isSubscribed = false; // Demo mode
    }

    bindEvents() {
        // Timeframe selection
        const timeframeSelect = document.getElementById('timeframe-select');
        if (timeframeSelect) {
            timeframeSelect.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                this.updateTimeframe(e.target.value);
            });
        }

        // Subscription activation
        document.querySelectorAll('.pricing-option button').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                const plan = e.target.closest('.pricing-option').querySelector('h4').textContent;
                this.activateSubscription(plan);
            });
        });
    }

    loadDemoMetrics() {
        // Simulate loading live metrics
        setTimeout(() => {
            this.updateMetric('market-size', '$402.5B', '+8.7% YoY growth');
            this.updateMetric('market-trend', 'Positive', 'Steady expansion');
            
            // Simulate competitor data
            this.updateCompetitors([
                { name: 'Coursera', share: '18.3%', trend: '‚Üë' },
                { name: 'LinkedIn Learning', share: '15.7%', trend: '‚Üí' },
                { name: 'Udemy', share: '12.4%', trend: '‚Üì' }
            ]);

            // Simulate recommendations
            this.updateRecommendations([
                'Expand SME segment with tiered pricing',
                'Develop AI-powered skills assessment',
                'Focus on emerging markets localization'
            ]);
        }, 1500);
    }

    updateMetric(metricId, value, trend) {
        const element = document.getElementById(metricId);
        if (element) {
            element.textContent = value;
            
            const trendElement = document.getElementById(metricId + '-trend');
            if (trendElement) {
                trendElement.textContent = trend;
            }
        }
    }

    updateCompetitors(competitors) {
        const listElement = document.getElementById('competitor-list');
        if (listElement) {
            listElement.innerHTML = competitors.map(comp => `
                <div class="competitor-item">
                    <span class="competitor-name">${comp.name}</span>
                    <span class="competitor-share">${comp.share}</span>
                    <span class="competitor-trend ${comp.trend === '‚Üë' ? 'up' : comp.trend === '‚Üì' ? 'down' : 'neutral'}">
                        ${comp.trend}
                    </span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        }
    }

    updateRecommendations(recommendations) {
        const listElement = document.getElementById('recommendations-list');
        if (listElement) {
            listElement.innerHTML = recommendations.map(rec => `
                <div class="recommendation-item">
                    <span class="recommendation-icon">üí°</span>
                    <span class="recommendation-text">${rec}</span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        }
    }

    refreshMetrics() {
        this.showNotification('Refreshing market data...');
        this.loadDemoMetrics();
    }

    updateTimeframe(timeframe) {
        this.showNotification(`Timeframe updated to: ${timeframe}`);
        // In production: Reload metrics for selected timeframe
    }

    activateSubscription(plan) {
        if (!this.isSubscribed) {
            window.open('../landing-ai-solutions/', '_blank');
            this.showNotification('Please complete analysis purchase first to activate monitoring');
        } else {
            this.showNotification(`Subscription activated: ${plan} plan`);
        }
    }

    showNotification(message) {
        // Same notification system as profile landing
        const notification = document.createElement('div');
        notification.style.cssText = `
            position: fixed;
            top: 20px;
            right: 20px;
            background: var(--matrix-accent);
            color: var(--matrix-bg);
            padding: 1rem 1.5rem;
            border-radius: 8px;
            z-index: 10000;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 25px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
        `;
        notification.textContent = message;
        document.body.appendChild(notification);
        
        setTimeout(() => {
            document.body.removeChild(notification);
        }, 5000);
    }
}

// Initialize when DOM is loaded
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    window.pulseDashboard = new PulseDashboard();
});

// Global functions for HTML onclick handlers
function refreshMetrics() {
    window.pulseDashboard.refreshMetrics();
}

function activateSubscription(plan) {
    window.pulseDashboard.activateSubscription(plan);
}

üìÑ 2. –§–ê–ô–õ: matrix-pulse/js/live-metrics.js
javascript
// Matrix Pulse - Live Metrics Engine
class LiveMetricsEngine {
    constructor() {
        this.metricsData = {};
        this.updateInterval = null;
        this.isDemoMode = true;
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.loadInitialMetrics();
        this.startAutoUpdates();
        this.setupChartPlaceholders();
    }

    loadInitialMetrics() {
        // Simulate API data loading
        setTimeout(() => {
            this.metricsData = {
                marketOverview: {
                    size: '$402.5B',
                    growth: '+8.7% YoY',
                    trend: 'positive',
                    segments: {
                        corporate: '$186.3B',
                        education: '$124.8B',
                        government: '$91.4B'
                    }
                },
                competitors: [
                    { name: 'Coursera', share: '18.3%', trend: 'up', change: '+2.1%' },
                    { name: 'LinkedIn Learning', share: '15.7%', trend: 'neutral', change: '+0.5%' },
                    { name: 'Udemy', share: '12.4%', trend: 'down', change: '-1.2%' },
                    { name: 'Docebo', share: '5.6%', trend: 'up', change: '+3.4%' },
                    { name: '360Learning', share: '4.2%', trend: 'up', change: '+0.8%' }
                ],
                customerInsights: {
                    enterprise: '42%',
                    smb: '35%',
                    education: '23%'
                },
                recommendations: [
                    'Expand SME segment with tiered pricing models',
                    'Develop AI-powered personalized learning paths',
                    'Strengthen partnerships with HR tech platforms',
                    'Focus on emerging markets in Asia-Pacific region',
                    'Enhance mobile learning experience capabilities'
                ]
            };

            this.updateAllMetrics();
            this.showNotification('Live metrics loaded successfully');
        }, 1000);
    }

    updateAllMetrics() {
        this.updateMarketOverview();
        this.updateCompetitiveLandscape();
        this.updateCustomerInsights();
        this.updateStrategicRecommendations();
    }

    updateMarketOverview() {
        const data = this.metricsData.marketOverview;
        
        this.updateMetricElement('market-size', data.size);
        this.updateMetricElement('market-trend', data.growth);
        
        // Update market chart placeholder
        const chartElement = document.getElementById('market-chart');
        if (chartElement) {
            chartElement.innerHTML = `
                <div style="text-align: center; padding: 1rem;">
                    <div style="font-size: 0.8rem; opacity: 0.8;">Market Segments</div>
                    <div style="display: flex; justify-content: center; gap: 1rem; margin-top: 0.5rem;">
                        <div style="text-align: center;">
                            <div style="font-weight: bold; color: #00dc82;">Corporate</div>
                            <div style="font-size: 0.8rem;">${data.segments.corporate}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div style="text-align: center;">
                            <div style="font-weight: bold; color: #00b4ff;">Education</div>
                            <div style="font-size: 0.8rem;">${data.segments.education}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }
    }

    updateCompetitiveLandscape() {
        const competitors = this.metricsData.competitors;
        const listElement = document.getElementById('competitor-list');
        
        if (listElement) {
            listElement.innerHTML = competitors.map(comp => `
                <div class="competitor-item">
                    <span class="competitor-name">${comp.name}</span>
                    <span class="competitor-share">${comp.share}</span>
                    <span class="competitor-trend ${comp.trend}">
                        ${comp.change}
                    </span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        }
    }

    updateCustomerInsights() {
        const insights = this.metricsData.customerInsights;
        const chartElement = document.getElementById('segmentation-chart');
        
        if (chartElement) {
            chartElement.innerHTML = `
                <div style="text-align: center; padding: 1rem;">
                    <div style="font-size: 0.8rem; opacity: 0.8; margin-bottom: 1rem;">Customer Segmentation</div>
                    <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 0.5rem;">
                        <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center;">
                            <span>Enterprise</span>
                            <span style="color: #00dc82; font-weight: bold;">${insights.enterprise}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center;">
                            <span>SMB</span>
                            <span style="color: #00b4ff; font-weight: bold;">${insights.smb}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center;">
                            <span>Education</span>
                            <span style="color: #8b5cf6; font-weight: bold;">${insights.education}</span>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }
    }

    updateStrategicRecommendations() {
        const recommendations = this.metricsData.recommendations;
        const listElement = document.getElementById('recommendations-list');
        
        if (listElement) {
            listElement.innerHTML = recommendations.map(rec => `
                <div class="recommendation-item">
                    <span class="recommendation-icon">üí°</span>
                    <span class="recommendation-text">${rec}</span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        }
    }

    updateMetricElement(elementId, value) {
        const element = document.getElementById(elementId);
        if (element) {
            // Add update animation
            element.style.opacity = '0.5';
            setTimeout(() => {
                element.textContent = value;
                element.style.opacity = '1';
            }, 300);
        }
    }

    startAutoUpdates() {
        // Simulate real-time updates every 30 seconds
        this.updateInterval = setInterval(() => {
            if (this.isDemoMode) {
                this.simulateLiveUpdate();
            }
        }, 30000);
    }

    simulateLiveUpdate() {
        // Simulate small data fluctuations for demo
        const randomCompetitor = Math.floor(Math.random() * this.metricsData.competitors.length);
        const changes = ['+0.1%', '+0.2%', '-0.1%', '+0.3%'];
        const randomChange = changes[Math.floor(Math.random() * changes.length)];
        
        this.metricsData.competitors[randomCompetitor].change = randomChange;
        
        this.updateCompetitiveLandscape();
        this.showNotification('Market data updated automatically');
    }

    setupChartPlaceholders() {
        // Initialize any chart placeholders
        console.log('Chart placeholders initialized');
    }

    refreshData() {
        this.showNotification('Manual refresh initiated...');
        
        // Simulate API call
        setTimeout(() => {
            this.loadInitialMetrics();
            this.showNotification('Data refreshed successfully');
        }, 1500);
    }

    changeTimeframe(timeframe) {
        this.showNotification(`Timeframe changed to: ${timeframe}`);
        
        // In production: Reload data for selected timeframe
        setTimeout(() => {
            this.loadInitialMetrics();
        }, 1000);
    }

    showNotification(message) {
        if (window.pulseDashboard && typeof window.pulseDashboard.showNotification === 'function') {
            window.pulseDashboard.showNotification(message);
        } else {
            // Fallback notification
            console.log('Matrix Pulse:', message);
        }
    }

    destroy() {
        if (this.updateInterval) {
            clearInterval(this.updateInterval);
        }
    }
}

// Initialize when DOM is loaded
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    window.liveMetrics = new LiveMetricsEngine();
});

// Global functions for metric interactions
function refreshMetricsData() {
    if (window.liveMetrics) {
        window.liveMetrics.refreshData();
    }
}

function changeMetricsTimeframe(timeframe) {
    if (window.liveMetrics) {
        window.liveMetrics.changeTimeframe(timeframe);
    }
}

    ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ executive-summary.md      # –ö—Ä–∞—Ç–∫–∞—è –≤–µ—Ä—Å–∏—è
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ üé® styles/
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ pdf-styles.css           # –°—Ç–∏–ª–∏ –¥–ª—è PDF
    ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ cover-page.css           # –¢–∏—Ç—É–ª—å–Ω–∞—è —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü–∞
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ üîß scripts/

    ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ fill-template.js         # –ó–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ —à–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω–∞

‚ö° –°–ö–†–ò–ü–¢ –î–õ–Ø –ê–í–¢–û–ú–ê–¢–ò–ß–ï–°–ö–û–ô –ì–ï–ù–ï–†–ê–¶–ò–ò:
üìÑ generate-pdf.js:
javascript
const fs = require('fs');
const { exec } = require('child_process');

class PDFGenerator {
    constructor() {
        this.templatePath = './templates/market-analysis.md';
        this.stylesPath = './styles/pdf-styles.css';
    }

    async generateReport(clientData, outputPath) {
        try {
            // 1. –ó–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è–µ–º —à–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞
            const filledTemplate = this.fillTemplate(clientData);
            
            // 2. –°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω—è–µ–º –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª
            const tempMd = `./temp/${clientData.company}-report.md`;
            fs.writeFileSync(tempMd, filledTemplate);
            
            // 3. –ö–æ–Ω–≤–µ—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –≤ PDF
            await this.convertToPDF(tempMd, outputPath);
            
            // 4. –ß–∏—Å—Ç–∏–º –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ã
            fs.unlinkSync(tempMd);
            
            console.log(`‚úÖ PDF –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω: ${outputPath}`);
            return outputPath;
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('‚ùå –û—à–∏–±–∫–∞ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ PDF:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    fillTemplate(clientData) {
        let template = fs.readFileSync(this.templatePath, 'utf8');
        
        // –ó–∞–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º –ø–µ—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤ —à–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω–µ
        const variables = {
            '{{company_name}}': clientData.company,
            '{{industry}}': clientData.industry,
            '{{date}}': new Date().toLocaleDateString(),
            '{{total_market_size}}': clientData.marketSize || 'N/A',
            '{{executive_summary}}': clientData.summary || 'Analysis in progress...'
        };
        
        Object.entries(variables).forEach(([key, value]) => {
            template = template.replace(new RegExp(key, 'g'), value);
        });
        
        return template;
    }

    convertToPDF(mdFilePath, outputPath) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const command = `pandoc "${mdFilePath}" -o "${outputPath}" --pdf-engine=wkhtmltopdf --css="${this.stylesPath}" --highlight-style=tango`;
            
            exec(command, (error, stdout, stderr) => {
                if (error) {
                    reject(`Pandoc error: ${stderr}`);
                } else {
                    resolve(stdout);
                }
            });
        });
    }
}

// –ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ:
const generator = new PDFGenerator();

const clientData = {
    company: '360Learning',
    industry: 'L&D Technology', 
    marketSize: '$402.5B',
    summary: 'Strong growth potential in SME segment with AI integration opportunities...'
};

generator.generateReport(clientData, './outputs/360learning-report.pdf');

‚ö° 5. –§–ê–ô–õ: pdf-generator/scripts/generate-pdf.js
javascript
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { exec } = require('child_process');
const util = require('util');

const execPromise = util.promisify(exec);

class PDFGenerator {
    constructor() {
        this.templatesDir = path.join(__dirname, '../templates');
        this.stylesDir = path.join(__dirname, '../styles');
        this.tempDir = path.join(__dirname, '../temp');
        this.outputsDir = path.join(__dirname, '../outputs');
        
        // –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º—ã–µ –ø–∞–ø–∫–∏
        this.ensureDirectories();
    }

    ensureDirectories() {
        [this.tempDir, this.outputsDir].forEach(dir => {
            if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) {
                fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });
            }
        });
    }

    async generateReport(clientData, templateName = 'market-analysis') {
        try {
            console.log(`üîÑ –ì–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–∞ –¥–ª—è: ${clientData.company}`);
            
            // 1. –ó–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–∞–µ–º –∏ –∑–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è–µ–º —à–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω
            const filledTemplate = await this.fillTemplate(templateName, clientData);
            
            // 2. –°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω—è–µ–º –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π Markdown —Ñ–∞–π–ª
            const tempMdPath = path.join(this.tempDir, `${clientData.company}-${Date.now()}.md`);
            fs.writeFileSync(tempMdPath, filledTemplate);
            
            // 3. –ì–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä—É–µ–º PDF
            const outputPdfPath = path.join(this.outputsDir, `${clientData.company}-market-report.pdf`);
            await this.convertToPDF(tempMdPath, outputPdfPath);
            
            // 4. –ß–∏—Å—Ç–∏–º –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ã
            fs.unlinkSync(tempMdPath);
            
            console.log(`‚úÖ PDF –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω: ${outputPdfPath}`);
            return outputPdfPath;
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('‚ùå –û—à–∏–±–∫–∞ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ PDF:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async fillTemplate(templateName, clientData) {
        const templatePath = path.join(this.templatesDir, `${templateName}.md`);
        
        if (!fs.existsSync(templatePath)) {
            throw new Error(`–®–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω –Ω–µ –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ–Ω: ${templatePath}`);
        }
        
        let template = fs.readFileSync(templatePath, 'utf8');
        
        // –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω—ã–µ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ
        const defaultVars = {
            '{{date}}': new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 
                year: 'numeric', 
                month: 'long', 
                day: 'numeric' 
            }),
            '{{report_date}}': new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0],
            '{{data_sources_count}}': '200+',
            '{{analysis_period}}': 'Q3 2024 - Q2 2025',
            '{{timeframe}}': 'Real-time + 12 months historical'
        };
        
        // –û–±—ä–µ–¥–∏–Ω—è–µ–º —Å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞
        const allVariables = { ...defaultVars, ...clientData };
        
        // –ó–∞–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º –≤—Å–µ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤ —à–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω–µ
        Object.entries(allVariables).forEach(([key, value]) => {
            const regex = new RegExp(this.escapeRegExp(key), 'g');
            template = template.replace(regex, value || 'N/A');
        });
        
        return template;
    }

    async convertToPDF(mdFilePath, outputPath) {
        const stylesPath = path.join(this.stylesDir, 'pdf-styles.css');
        
        const command = [
            'pandoc',
            `"${mdFilePath}"`,
            '-o', `"${outputPath}"`,
            '--pdf-engine=wkhtmltopdf',
            '--css', `"${stylesPath}"`,
            '--highlight-style=tango',
            '--toc',
            '--toc-depth=3',
            '--number-sections',
            '-V', 'papersize:a4',
            '-V', 'geometry:margin=2cm'
        ].join(' ');
        
        try {
            const { stdout, stderr } = await execPromise(command);
            if (stderr) console.warn('Pandoc warnings:', stderr);
            return stdout;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Pandoc conversion failed: ${error.stderr}`);
        }
    }

    escapeRegExp(string) {
        return string.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
    }

    // –í—Å–ø–æ–º–æ–≥–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–∞—è —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—è –¥–ª—è –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–π –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏
    async quickGenerate(company, industry, summary) {
        const clientData = {
            company_name: company,
            company: company,
            industry: industry,
            executive_summary: summary,
            total_market_size: 'To be analyzed',
            market_growth: 'Growing',
            immediate_opportunities: 'AI integration, Market expansion',
            key_recommendations: 'Conduct deeper market analysis'
        };
        
        return await this.generateReport(clientData);
    }
}

// –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è
async function example() {
    const generator = new PDFGenerator();
    
    const clientData = {
        company_name: '360Learning',
        company: '360Learning',
        industry: 'L&D Technology',
        executive_summary: 'Strong growth potential in SME segment with significant opportunities for AI integration and market expansion in emerging regions.',
        total_market_size: '$402.5B',
        market_growth: '+8.7% CAGR',
        immediate_opportunities: 'SME segment expansion, AI-powered personalization, Emerging markets',
        key_recommendations: 'Develop tiered pricing for SMEs, Enhance AI capabilities, Focus on Asia-Pacific growth'
    };
    
    try {
        const pdfPath = await generator.generateReport(clientData);
        console.log('üéâ –û—Ç—á–µ—Ç –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤:', pdfPath);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('üí• –û—à–∏–±–∫–∞:', error.message);
    }
}

// –ó–∞–ø—É—Å–∫ –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä–∞ –µ—Å–ª–∏ —Ñ–∞–π–ª –≤—ã–∑–≤–∞–Ω –Ω–∞–ø—Ä—è–º—É—é
if (require.main === module) {
    example();
}

module.exports = PDFGenerator;

markdown
‚úÖ **–ì–û–¢–û–í–û:**
- –ü–æ–ª–Ω–∞—è –∞—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞
- 2 –ª–µ–Ω–¥–∏–Ω–≥–∞ (–ø—Ä–æ—Ñ–∏–ª—å–Ω—ã–π + –º–æ–Ω–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–Ω–≥)
- –°–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ PDF –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–æ–≤
- –í—Å—è –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—è –∏ —à–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω—ã

üîÑ **–û–ñ–ò–î–ê–ï–¢:**

const fs = require('fs');

class SimplePDFGenerator {
    static generateQuickReport(clientData) {
        // 1. –ß–∏—Ç–∞–µ–º —à–∞–±–ª–æ–Ω
        let template = fs.readFileSync('./templates/market-analysis.md', 'utf8');
        
        // 2. –ó–∞–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º –ø–µ—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ
        template = template
            .replace(/{{company_name}}/g, clientData.company)
            .replace(/{{industry}}/g, clientData.industry)
            .replace(/{{executive_summary}}/g, clientData.summary)
            .replace(/{{date}}/g, new Date().toLocaleDateString());
        
        // 3. –°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω—è–µ–º –∑–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª
        const outputFile = `./outputs/${clientData.company}-report.md`;
        fs.writeFileSync(outputFile, template);
        
        console.log(`‚úÖ –û—Ç—á–µ—Ç –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤: ${outputFile}`);
        console.log('üìã –°–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–º–æ–µ:');
        console.log('---');
        console.log(template.substring(0, 500) + '...');
        console.log('---');
        
        return outputFile;
    }
}

// –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è

üîß 4. –§–ê–ô–õ: landing-ai-solutions/js/main.js
javascript
// Landing AI Solutions - Main Controller
class LandingAISolutions {
    constructor() {
        this.selectedFormat = null;
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.bindEvents();
        this.setupSmoothScroll();
    }

    bindEvents() {
        // Format selection
        document.querySelectorAll('.format-card button').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                const card = e.target.closest('.format-card');
                const format = card.querySelector('h3').textContent;
                this.selectFormat(format);
            });
        });

        // Payment confirmation
        const confirmBtn = document.querySelector('.btn-confirm');
        if (confirmBtn) {
            confirmBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                this.showConfirmationForm();
            });
        }

        // Copy address button
        const copyBtn = document.querySelector('.btn-copy');
        if (copyBtn) {
            copyBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                this.copyAddress();
            });
        }
    }

    setupSmoothScroll() {
        // Smooth scrolling for navigation links
        document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
            anchor.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                const target = document.querySelector(this.getAttribute('href'));
                if (target) {
                    target.scrollIntoView({
                        behavior: 'smooth',
                        block: 'start'
                    });
                }
            });
        });
    }

    requestDemo() {
        const company = prompt('Please enter your company name:');
        const email = prompt('Please enter your email for demo delivery:');
        
        if (company && email) {
            this.submitDemoRequest(company, email);
        }
    }

    submitDemoRequest(company, email) {
        const requestData = {
            company: company,
            email: email,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            source: 'landing_ai_solutions'
        };

        console.log('Demo request submitted:', requestData);
        this.showNotification('Demo request received! We will contact you within 24 hours.');
        
        // Simulate demo delivery
        setTimeout(() => {
            this.deliverDemoReport(company, email);
        }, 2000);
    }

    deliverDemoReport(company, email) {
        const demoContent = this.generateDemoContent(company);
        
        // Simulate email delivery
        console.log('Demo report delivered to:', email);
        this.showNotification(`Demo report sent to ${email}! Check your inbox.`);
    }

    generateDemoContent(company) {
        return {
            company: company,
            sections: [
                "Market Overview Analysis",
                "Competitive Landscape", 
                "Target Audience Insights",
                "Strategic Recommendations",
                "Implementation Roadmap"
            ],
            generated: new Date().toISOString()
        };
    }

    selectFormat(format) {
        this.selectedFormat = format;
        this.scrollToSection('payment');
        this.showNotification(`Selected: ${format}. Proceed to payment when ready.`);
    }

    copyAddress() {
        const address = document.getElementById('usdt-address').textContent;
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(address).then(() => {
            this.showNotification('USDT address copied to clipboard!');
        }).catch(() => {
            // Fallback for older browsers
            const textArea = document.createElement('textarea');
            textArea.value = address;
            document.body.appendChild(textArea);
            textArea.select();
            document.execCommand('copy');
            document.body.removeChild(textArea);
            this.showNotification('USDT address copied to clipboard!');
        });
    }

    showConfirmationForm() {
        const txHash = prompt('Please enter your USDT transaction hash:');
        const email = prompt('Please enter your email for report delivery:');
        
        if (txHash && email) {
            this.confirmPayment(txHash, email);
        }
    }

    confirmPayment(txHash, email) {
        const paymentData = {
            format: this.selectedFormat,
            txHash: txHash,
            email: email,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        };

        console.log('Payment confirmed:', paymentData);
        this.showNotification('Payment confirmed! Full report will be delivered within 48 hours.');
    }

    scrollToSection(sectionId) {
        const element = document.getElementById(sectionId);
        if (element) {
            element.scrollIntoView({
                behavior: 'smooth',
                block: 'start'
            });
        }
    }

    showNotification(message) {
        // Create notification element
        const notification = document.createElement('div');
        notification.style.cssText = `
            position: fixed;
            top: 20px;
            right: 20px;
            background: var(--matrix-accent);
            color: var(--matrix-bg);
            padding: 1rem 1.5rem;
            border-radius: 8px;
            z-index: 10000;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 25px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
            font-weight: 600;
            max-width: 300px;
            word-wrap: break-word;
        `;
        notification.textContent = message;
        document.body.appendChild(notification);
        
        // Remove after 5 seconds
        setTimeout(() => {
            if (notification.parentNode) {
                notification.parentNode.removeChild(notification);
            }
        }, 5000);
    }
}

// Initialize when DOM is loaded
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    window.landingAI = new LandingAISolutions();
});

// Global functions for HTML onclick handlers
function requestDemo() {
    if (window.landingAI) {
        window.landingAI.requestDemo();
    }
}

function scrollToSection(sectionId) {
    if (window.landingAI) {
        window.landingAI.scrollToSection(sectionId);
    }
}

function selectFormat(format) {
    if (window.landingAI) {
        window.landingAI.selectFormat(format);
    }
}

function copyAddress() {
    if (window.landingAI) {
        window.landingAI.copyAddress();
    }
}

function showConfirmationForm() {
    if (window.landingAI) {
        window.landingAI.showConfirmationForm();
    }
}
üí≥ 5. –§–ê–ô–õ: landing-ai-solutions/js/payment.js
javascript
// Payment-specific functionality
class PaymentSystem {
    constructor() {
        this.paymentMethods = ['USDT (TRC20)'];
        this.currentMethod = 'USDT (TRC20)';
    }

    validatePayment(txHash) {
        // Basic validation - in production, integrate with blockchain explorer API
        if (!txHash || txHash.length < 64) {
            return { valid: false, error: 'Invalid transaction hash' };
        }
        
        return { valid: true, transaction: txHash };
    }

    simulatePaymentConfirmation(txHash) {
        return new Promise((resolve) => {
            setTimeout(() => {
                resolve({
                    confirmed: true,
                    txHash: txHash,
                    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                    blocks: Math.floor(Math.random() * 10) + 1
                });
            }, 2000);
        });
    }

    generatePaymentInstructions(method) {
        const instructions = {
            'USDT (TRC20)': {
                network: 'TRON (TRC20)',
                address: 'TGvyTtKBiSY5RHsfWipRdTjpWroeQSGLTC',
                memo: 'Optional: Your email for report delivery',
                confirmation: 'Usually 2-5 minutes'
            }
        };
        
        return instructions[method] || instructions['USDT (TRC20)'];
    }
}

// Initialize payment system
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    window.paymentSystem = new PaymentSystem();
});

/* Matrix Intelligence Design System */
:root {

}
